text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-brNrDLCpkVs/TsE_hVdBdbI/AAAAAAAAITA/x8XG1Yk9jks/s1600/imagesCA1XRDN9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-brNrDLCpkVs/TsE_hVdBdbI/AAAAAAAAITA/x8XG1Yk9jks/s1600/imagesCA1XRDN9.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nYou could see they have been doing it for years as the raised hand was shrivelled. Yet their glowing faces showed absolute bliss. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8MOGHbfI0b0/TsFqU1IJUqI/AAAAAAAAIYo/A3p026er7kE/s1600/imagesCA6ANFDB.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8MOGHbfI0b0/TsFqU1IJUqI/AAAAAAAAIYo/A3p026er7kE/s1600/imagesCA6ANFDB.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SI6qEojcUbE/TsFqxWHwC3I/AAAAAAAAIYw/j0VYeNj0NGM/s1600/imagesCA3O32JZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SI6qEojcUbE/TsFqxWHwC3I/AAAAAAAAIYw/j0VYeNj0NGM/s1600/imagesCA3O32JZ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-jQlKLYaqAVw/TsFq10B4N1I/AAAAAAAAIY4/FDFnpY-Orzs/s1600/imagesCAXCN9BH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-jQlKLYaqAVw/TsFq10B4N1I/AAAAAAAAIY4/FDFnpY-Orzs/s1600/imagesCAXCN9BH.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-z_StPrKHM8k/TsM0KgHg8HI/AAAAAAAAIlw/9aUvyjYjDeM/s1600/imagesCA5G0S2E.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-z_StPrKHM8k/TsM0KgHg8HI/AAAAAAAAIlw/9aUvyjYjDeM/s1600/imagesCA5G0S2E.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FUFtkIJ0j28/Tr7X0FX6gZI/AAAAAAAAII4/TeYwPV34TeU/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FUFtkIJ0j28/Tr7X0FX6gZI/AAAAAAAAII4/TeYwPV34TeU/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mnfZoFBqvXw/TsFphxSt8kI/AAAAAAAAIYQ/D89NJ2L5RJo/s1600/imagesCAOAMZA9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mnfZoFBqvXw/TsFphxSt8kI/AAAAAAAAIYQ/D89NJ2L5RJo/s1600/imagesCAOAMZA9.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5x2O4f7rYXI/TsFpoThYBbI/AAAAAAAAIYY/vwKoT3E62aM/s1600/imagesCALQPJA7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5x2O4f7rYXI/TsFpoThYBbI/AAAAAAAAIYY/vwKoT3E62aM/s1600/imagesCALQPJA7.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_mFrvEkYhY0/TsFpuMp5z5I/AAAAAAAAIYg/cycs5S1qK6I/s1600/imagesCAJ3WIP4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_mFrvEkYhY0/TsFpuMp5z5I/AAAAAAAAIYg/cycs5S1qK6I/s1600/imagesCAJ3WIP4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThis frightened and totally demoralised his soldiers and even their horses. They literally shat in their pants. &nbsp;The battle with King Porus was half lost , there itself.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_7FzXM2TPwM/T6uiQt1ISlI/AAAAAAAAK7U/zFc1b-1aXAQ/s1600/tumblr_m1pk4yPftr1r4esjjo1_500.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"383\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_7FzXM2TPwM/T6uiQt1ISlI/AAAAAAAAK7U/zFc1b-1aXAQ/s400/tumblr_m1pk4yPftr1r4esjjo1_500.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZGIr5xFgoT8/Tr9BrHGBOJI/AAAAAAAAIN4/Ry6hZKJ7jYc/s1600/imagesCAHTP5I0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZGIr5xFgoT8/Tr9BrHGBOJI/AAAAAAAAIN4/Ry6hZKJ7jYc/s1600/imagesCAHTP5I0.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAfter that Alexander made sure his soldiers never saw these gruesome sights.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cdynwYIpuzU/Tr7YB2ADCKI/AAAAAAAAIJA/VigsVZFwWxA/s1600/imagesCA76JQYJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cdynwYIpuzU/Tr7YB2ADCKI/AAAAAAAAIJA/VigsVZFwWxA/s1600/imagesCA76JQYJ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\">What compels me to write, is that the&nbsp;7000 year old Rig Veda, written in Sanskrit,&nbsp;has 117 hymns about a wonder&nbsp;elexir by the name of Soma.&nbsp; And thousands of temples have the Samudra Manthan depicted , extracting amrit by churning&nbsp;the ocean &nbsp;. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\">Till today no body has got it right, in any book or any post on the Internet. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-i-YtS0pxrB8/Tr7aumLZmGI/AAAAAAAAIL4/9_57xiuiAnQ/s1600/imagesCAHC0N4L.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-i-YtS0pxrB8/Tr7aumLZmGI/AAAAAAAAIL4/9_57xiuiAnQ/s1600/imagesCAHC0N4L.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nLet me first narrate&nbsp;the Hindu mythological story first.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kOOsJjdCL0E/Tr7ambHrhzI/AAAAAAAAILw/LZaLqvrpXRk/s1600/imagesCA3WYVG9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kOOsJjdCL0E/Tr7ambHrhzI/AAAAAAAAILw/LZaLqvrpXRk/s1600/imagesCA3WYVG9.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe king of Gods ( Devas ) Indra was a bit of a egomaniac.&nbsp; Once he was riding on his elephant Airavata when he bumped into a seer Durvasa Muni on the way, who was famous for his short fuse. Everybody was in awe&nbsp;of Durvasa, and he always wore tattered clothes due to a vow of insanity he was observing. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LlWFrJK-TbY/Tr7agzvWBrI/AAAAAAAAILo/Lw6RSIa5GFs/s1600/imagesCAH2P9IE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LlWFrJK-TbY/Tr7agzvWBrI/AAAAAAAAILo/Lw6RSIa5GFs/s1600/imagesCAH2P9IE.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nHe had with him a garland of heavenly flowers given to him by a nymph. He tossed the garland towards Indra who placed it on his elephants head showing total insensitivity. The elephant was disturbed by the strange scent of the flowers and it threw down the garland on the ground and stamped on it. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3wwGynmvILU/Tr7aa0dqXYI/AAAAAAAAILg/agQV-Fvi4hI/s1600/imagesCA76JQYJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3wwGynmvILU/Tr7aa0dqXYI/AAAAAAAAILg/agQV-Fvi4hI/s1600/imagesCA76JQYJ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nDurvasa was upset seeing the disrespect and cursed Indra, and told him that he would be thrown down from his throne, the same way the garland was thrown down..He also cursed all the&nbsp;Devas and said that they would soon lose their sheen. &nbsp;Indra immediately got down from the elephant and begged for forgiveness,by Durvasa would not retract the curse or even soften it, and went on his way.. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0b1mdsApeUE/Tr7aVJ_0uJI/AAAAAAAAILY/QYE8ugbyKS0/s1600/imagesCAUDD2QU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0b1mdsApeUE/Tr7aVJ_0uJI/AAAAAAAAILY/QYE8ugbyKS0/s1600/imagesCAUDD2QU.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nWhen the Asuras ( demons ) heard of this they were overjoyed, and they attacked the Devas under the leadership of Bali, (the King of Kerala ). The Devas were routed in battle and Bali became king of the universe. The gods were told by Brahma to go to Vishnu for help.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MUSyG0iy9YE/Tr7aOS5c7DI/AAAAAAAAILQ/j4mCXdHXkPg/s1600/imagesCAEBSSYS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MUSyG0iy9YE/Tr7aOS5c7DI/AAAAAAAAILQ/j4mCXdHXkPg/s1600/imagesCAEBSSYS.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nVishnu told them to strike a deal with the Asuras, and get them to join them as a team to churn amrit or ambrosia ( nectar of immortality ) from the oceans, and promise to share it 50-50 with them..It was done long ago in the past at the end of the last precession cycle ( 25675 years cycle ) &nbsp;.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GZlyHW-f-Xk/Tr821vVwcSI/AAAAAAAAIMw/EQ3GyNyQ1YQ/s1600/imagesCAFI8PYZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GZlyHW-f-Xk/Tr821vVwcSI/AAAAAAAAIMw/EQ3GyNyQ1YQ/s1600/imagesCAFI8PYZ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAnd Vishnu would make sure that Asuras would NOT get a drop of it. There was no other alternative as Sage Shukracharya the son of Bhrigu Rishi was on the side of the Asuras and was training them.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Gd66nivcF1I/Tr7aHlUbc9I/AAAAAAAAILI/mNEH0uI1lXU/s1600/imagesCAD8YL21.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Gd66nivcF1I/Tr7aHlUbc9I/AAAAAAAAILI/mNEH0uI1lXU/s1600/imagesCAD8YL21.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nShukracharya had a point to prove to the Devas who had spurned him when he offered to be their guru. They chose Sage Brihaspati son of Maharishi Angira instead. Brihaspati is known in other cultures as Zeus&nbsp; or Thor.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rDmc0LvfjjA/Tr7aBz0yeZI/AAAAAAAAILA/LsxtsXGp3RI/s1600/imagesCAIGBZ6T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rDmc0LvfjjA/Tr7aBz0yeZI/AAAAAAAAILA/LsxtsXGp3RI/s1600/imagesCAIGBZ6T.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nLord Shiva had a mantra&nbsp;by the name of Sanjeevani. This mantra was very powerful and could revive a dead man. He would give it only to those who pleased him. One way to please him was to hang upside down, on a high tree branch by your knees for one year. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-L523c0aN6S4/Tr7bFFlPYxI/AAAAAAAAIMQ/XQ6xxDg5N1U/s1600/imagesCAPTZV7H.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-L523c0aN6S4/Tr7bFFlPYxI/AAAAAAAAIMQ/XQ6xxDg5N1U/s1600/imagesCAPTZV7H.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIf you fall asleep and drop down you break you neck. You cannot talk and cannot consume food . Right below smoke would be sent up from a bonfire of dry leaves. Nobody dared to do this penance. Shukrachrya was determined to please Shiva and get hold of this mantra.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--mFdNIomoKk/Tr7Z7v8rDKI/AAAAAAAAIK4/0C1yBiav_sM/s1600/imagesCA0L9ACU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--mFdNIomoKk/Tr7Z7v8rDKI/AAAAAAAAIK4/0C1yBiav_sM/s1600/imagesCA0L9ACU.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nEverybody was keeping keen vigilance of this penance as the one year completion date was getting near. The King of the Devas Lord Indra panicked and decided to play a bit dirty. He sent his daughter disguised as a brahmin woman past the sentries. She threw some dry red &nbsp;chillies into the fire without anybody noticing. The acrid fumes of the chillies made Shukracharyas eyes bleed. The&nbsp;woman was filled with remorse. &nbsp;Lord Shiva unable to tolerate this foul play immediately appeared and gave Shukracharya the mantra as a boon.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-VrlPYIT0m7Y/Tr7Z0-cBf3I/AAAAAAAAIKw/Zz8-i4o_hhg/s1600/imagesCAVIKIZ2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-VrlPYIT0m7Y/Tr7Z0-cBf3I/AAAAAAAAIKw/Zz8-i4o_hhg/s1600/imagesCAVIKIZ2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThis churning of the ocean was an elaborate process. Mount Mandaranchal ( Meru ) was to be the churning dasher. Vasuki the King of serpents was to be the rope. Vishnu avatar Kurma a tortoise would take the rotating Meru on its back. Smart Indra told the gods to hold the tail . The dumb asuras held the head, and they started churning to and fro for all they were worth. Asuras were getting scorched by flames which appeared frequently from the mouth of 5 headed Vasuki.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0Xn_9UxDrrQ/Tr7Ztg1d9uI/AAAAAAAAIKo/ZidZWHgXzns/s1600/imagesCAEK0P1F.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0Xn_9UxDrrQ/Tr7Ztg1d9uI/AAAAAAAAIKo/ZidZWHgXzns/s1600/imagesCAEK0P1F.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nPretty soon Vasuki felt the strain and vomited out deadly venom, which became so toxic and polymerising forming a froth on the ocean , that all were scared.&nbsp; This would have been the end of the world.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Sr8jEjsEegc/Tr9g0KVtT-I/AAAAAAAAIOg/VMdC0_t3yi0/s1600/shivaratri6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Sr8jEjsEegc/Tr9g0KVtT-I/AAAAAAAAIOg/VMdC0_t3yi0/s320/shivaratri6.jpg\" width=\"253\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nLord Shiva was compassionate and drank up this poison. Shiva's consort Parvati pressed his neck so that the poison would not reach his stomach. Shiva did not die, but his neck became blue and hence his name Neel Kanthan.( blue throated ).. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/AD8zODCUofA/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/AD8zODCUofA&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/AD8zODCUofA&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nShiva was advised by the celestial doctors not to sleep, and keep dancing, so that the poison could be burnt out and excreted . The gods took turns to amuse Shiva throughout the long night. This night is a festival in India ( Shiva ratri -- or thanks giving night for Shiva ) were Hindus fast all day , do NOT sleep at night , and have cultural festivities in all temples.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.5pt; line-height: 115%;\">Below Dhanwantari in 4 armed Vishnu form -holding the Sudarsana Chakra weapon and Conch in the upper right and lefts hands. In the other two hands he carries a pot containing the nectar of immortality and a leech.</span></i><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Vq3Fjv8uJnM/Tr9jCfqa7vI/AAAAAAAAIOo/ck722jvLZ30/s1600/god_dhanwantari_wallpaper_nice.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Vq3Fjv8uJnM/Tr9jCfqa7vI/AAAAAAAAIOo/ck722jvLZ30/s320/god_dhanwantari_wallpaper_nice.jpg\" width=\"240\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">The 14th shloka of <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">Shivmahimna Stotra </span>says: \"O three eyed Lord, when the poison came up through the churning of the ocean by the gods and demons, they were all aghast with fear as if the untimely end of all creation was imminent. In your kindness, you drank all the poison that still makes your throat blue. O Lord, even this blue mark does but increase your glory. What is apparently a blemish becomes an ornament in one intent on ridding the world of fear.\"</span></i><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/CZDFI3tH9pU/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/CZDFI3tH9pU&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/CZDFI3tH9pU&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nFinally the churning was successful and Lord Dhanvantari , the god of Ayurveda rose from the ocean., with a pot containing the nectar of immortality or amrit. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>52.0 %</b></span><br /><br />capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</span></div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Harshil Shah<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">September 21, 2014 at\n9:06 AM<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pranam Guruji,<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Indeed, i read the\nabove post and its exactly same. , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Horizontal rows add to powers of 2 (i.e., 1, 2, 4, 8, 16, etc.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The horizontal rows represent powers of 11 (1, 11, 121, 1331, 14641) for the first 5 rows, in which the numbers have only a single digit.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Adding any two successive numbers in the diagonal 1-3-6-10-15-21-28\u2026 results in a perfect square (1, 4, 9, 16, etc.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">It can be used to find combinations in probability problems (if, for instance, you pick any two of five items, the number of possible combinations is 10, found by looking in the second place of the fifth row. Do not count the 1\u2019s.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">When the first number to the right of the 1 in any row is a prime number, all numbers in that row are divisible by that prime number</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The Fibonacci Series is found in Pascal\u2019s Triangle.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Pascal\u2019s Triangle, is formed by starting with an apex of 1. Every number below in the triangle is the sum of the two numbers diagonally above it to the left and the right, with positions outside the triangle counting as zero.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The numbers on diagonals of the Pascalstriangle add to the Fibonacci series</span><br /><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XMriWTvPXHI&amp;pbjreload=10</span></span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The Fibonacci numbers are--</span><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">0, 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 13, ... This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>52.0 %</b></span><br /><br />capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</span></div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Harshil Shah<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">September 21, 2014 at\n9:06 AM<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pranam Guruji,<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Indeed, i read the\nabove post and its exactly same. This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>52.0 %</b></span><br /><br />capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</span></div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Harshil Shah<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">September 21, 2014 at\n9:06 AM<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pranam Guruji,<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Indeed, i read the\nabove post and its exactly same. </span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; </span>Time/ Voyage charterers and shippers have limited powers to interfere with Master signing the bill of lading. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-VG-X-OR5Ibc/Trs72dkKZnI/AAAAAAAAH4Q/puA4MZDqd9I/s1600/imagesCAXQK6KG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"178\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-VG-X-OR5Ibc/Trs72dkKZnI/AAAAAAAAH4Q/puA4MZDqd9I/s400/imagesCAXQK6KG.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"font-size: x-large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">TIME CHARTER<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is usual for new ships to be chartered for a long period ,say for 10 years. Owner has to keep the vessel seaworthy, man her, insure her, and technically operate her as per agreed charter party parameters.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Charterers run the ship commercially in respect of cargoes, employment and give voyage orders. They pay for ships bunkers ( not lubes ) port expenses, agency fees, communication .<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>The time-charter hire is paid as a fixed rate per day, The shipowner does not get freight.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Then vessel may go off hire if the charter party performance is breached like engine, boiler failures, pollution detention or cargo-pump breakdowns. Speed and bunkers consumptions are specified in the C/P . Diversions due to accident , breakdown, for landing sick crew or for whatever causes vessel is responsible are on owners account. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>When sub chartered<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>by the Head time charterers , the Master is now acting both as the ship Head owners and Disponent owners representative. When the agent refers to the owner it is the Disponent owner. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Time-Charterers are responsible for all water used for tank cleaning water and boiler feed water. Owners are responsible for all water used for domestic reasons. Tank chemicals used for tank cleaning , Nitric acid for passivation , lab reagents for wall wash , rags, Scotch Brite pads, shoe covers etc is on the Time-Charterers account and should therefore be ordered through them.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: x-large;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-size: x-large;\">VOYAGE CHARTER<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -63.8pt;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On a voyage-charter, owners get money by way of freight in a lump sum. Owners do not get freight for anything loaded over the fixture.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Charterers do not get involved in the vessel\u2019s operation. Their only obligation is to deliver the cargo as described in the charter party to the vessel, and the loading and discharging is to be performed within the agreed time. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If the agreed time is exceeded a compensation called demurrage is payable to the Owner. However the ship should remain at charters disposal. In between this if you mindlessly bunker the ship demurrage cannot be claimed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Laytime continues till cargo documents come on board. The time of hose disconnection is important for vessels on voyage charter as the voyage ends there.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Sample of laytime demurrage notice :<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em>\u201c without prejudice to the owners claim for demurrage, this serves to notify you that according to my calculations the laytime of 72 hours stipulated in the C/P has been utilized on date/ hour, whereupon the vessel is now operating on demurrage\u201d signed master. Owners have lien upon cargo for freight, dead freight, demurrage, average and other charges.<o:p></o:p></em></span></div><em>  </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If the charterer does not load full cargo owner can claim deadfreight. Ensure the deadfreight is signed at the time of signing bill of lading. If the Charterers are unable to deliver a full cargo (or whatever minimum quantity has been agreed) Owners are entitled to dead-freight when there is draft restriction.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If the vessel is cubed out then it is on owners account<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Charterers pay for the transportation either by a lumpsum<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>or by a fixed rate per metric ton .<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If the freight is payable as a lumpsum, the agreed cargo capacity is at Charterers disposal and must be paid for whether used or not.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If freight is payable per metric ton of cargo loaded, the master must load maximum possible. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When the Voyage Charterer sub charters the ship the master must ensure that all instructions are in accordance with the original C/P, especially clauses like NAABSA. <o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On a voyage-charter, Head owners / Disponent owners pay for the bunkers and for most expenses relating to the port calls including communication and representation.<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Voyage charterer have option of subletting part or whole of vessel but remain responsible for payments---read your charter party in full .<o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A contract of affreightment</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> is usually based on voyage-charter terms . The contract covers a certain lumpsum quantity of cargo which is to be moved within a certain time frame. A contract of affreightment does not involve a specific named vessel.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Owners are free to use any suitable vessel and even to charter another ship.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-0OolfjHXxXo/Trs6-TZYqDI/AAAAAAAAH4A/4E3QuUVkfjA/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil+2.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em;
